            038E: draw_box_position $BAR_X $BAR_Y5 size $TEMP_BREATH $SLOW_MODE_SIZE2_Y RGBA $BREATH_R2 $BREATH_G2 $BREATH_B2 $HUD_ALPHA
            else
            gosub @CHECKFUCK
            end
        else        
        gosub @CHECKFUCK         
        end
    else

    end
